<review>When it comes to the Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street you NEED TO STOP AND TAKE A MINUTE TO THINK! And this is Why?
Because the Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street is like GRANDMA'S HOME its old and filled with MEMORIES OF LIFE GONE BYE. Take the time to NOTICE THE BEAUTY OF ITS STRUCTURE THAT HAS WITHSTOOD TIME.

STOP AND THINK OF ALL THE THOUSANDS OF PEOPLE WHO BEFORE YOU have come here to this very Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street to pickup their mail or dropped off their mail to family and friends so far away filled with hope and EXCITEMENT when the mail or package arrives can I still remember that feeling.

You need to REMEMBER YEARS AGO THERE WAS NO E-MAIL, TEXTING, FAXES OR TELEPHONES IN EVERY HOME but there was the MAIL and years ago people depended on the United States Postal Service to get the TREASURED MAIL OR PACKAGES THERE without fail and this Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street was apart it.

This Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street was the hub of Riverside where people would meet the neighbor or friends and socialized back then it was an EVENT AN ADVENTURE TO GO INTO TOWN and walk into this very Historic Post Office.

I was about 12 years old before I ever walked into the Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street back in the day I lived in what was known as the boonies and it was my first trip into downtown Riverside.

And yes our only reason for coming into town was to go to the United States Post Office on Orange Street to buy stamps and I was struck immeadiatly by the rich beauty of the wood the curve of the stairs, all the mailboxes, the large windows and back then the heaters worked and the warmth was wonderful I had never seen anything like it.

I remember you could walk upstairs and there were more people getting PASS PORTS and IMMIGRATION things done but it was MAGNIFICENT and the views out the window were a WONDER and EXCITEMENT to fill the heart it truely an ADVENTURE I never forgot.

There were people of all kinds coming and going and yes there the was a line but then you enjoyed having a polite conversation.

So next time you walk into the HISTORIC DOWNTOWN POST OFFICE remember you are entering the GRANDMOTHER of all Post Offices in Riverside County so RESPECT IT.

Just like your Grandmother's home you do not go there for the fast service or the lasted high tech you enter with your heart and enjoy the memories that have gone and the ones yet to come and you are a part of it.

So the next time you walk into the Riverside Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street and you place your hand on that door STOP AND APPRECIATE think about HOW MANY PEOPLE HAVE PUSHED THAT DOOR OPEN JUST AS YOU HAVE NOW and remind yourself you ARE entering  HISTORY and at the same time you are apart of history today.

To this day each time I walk into the Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street I MARVEL at the HISTORY AND BEAUTY think of all the men that labored at creating such a BEAUTIFULLY DESIGNED BUILDING. WITH SUCH CRAFTSMANSHIP IN THE DETAILS   that has stood the test of time.

The SERVICE maybe slow and not so EFFICIENT or up to your HIGH STANDARDS but just like GRANDMA we show RESPECT AND UNDERSTANDING AND PATIENTS BECAUSE our Riverside Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street has EARNED IT AND DESERVES IT.

The Riverside Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street  maybe old and moves slow but it is DEPENDABLE and SERVES MY NEEDS WITHOUT COMPLAINT.

And as for the Employees that work there and also the Caretakers for our Riverside Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street we say THANK YOU.

I will continue to go when I need postal service and wait in line even though there is no longer any polite conversations and WHY?

BECAUSE I NEVER WANT the Riverside Historic United States Post Office on Orange Street to think for on moment in time I DID NOT NEED HER OR I COULD DO WITHOUT HER AND WATCH AS THEY CLOSE HERE DOORS FOREVER.

Rebecca Velasquez</review>< user_name>

Another Dutch bros has arrived and if your in a long drive down or up 99 in the galt area it makes the drive a bit cooler or hotter depending on your drink of choice. Open 24 hours and right off the highway makes the spot easy to hit up.

< review>
Authorized but Incompetent

Summary: They couldn't figure out what the problem is but a local mechanic shop could. They even charged me 500$ for not finding the problem. I doubt about them even checking it out.

I have a 2013 Range Rover Evoque Pure.
My car was not starting so I got it diagnosed by a third party technician.
I was told that the starter was not working so we got the starter replaced. The starter I bought was a brand new one that was triple tested so that we knew that it was working. But after we got it replaced the car still didn't start.
So I thought that it would be better to bring the car to an Authorized dealer.
One would expect that an authorized dealer would be proficient at what they do.
On December 19 2019 I brought my car to the Land Rover Jaguar of Stevens Creek. I told them what happened and what the problem is. I told them that the starter is newly replaced. These remarks are already present on the service documents that they gave me.
After their diagnosis they told me that the starter was not working and it needs to be replaced. I didn't believe them because of my past experience and because of the fact that it was replaced just yet. So I took the car and brought it to a local mechanic shop.
They checked the car and told me that the problem was not the starter but  positive cable harness to the starter motor. They ordered new parts and replaced it. Right now everything works fine.</review>

< Text>
I met up with Mark and Jay to look into the possibility of making a purchase of a 2016 Range Rover LWB V8 Supercharger. I had a "wish list" of color, body style, equipment, etc. and they worked with me over a two day time period. They had nothing on their lot that matched my desires, so they both started computer searching other dealerships that might have one that they could get for me on a trade. They were able to fine one that matched my "wish list" 99%. Apparently, the long wheel base vehicles are few and far between and most dealerships do not like to trade them off their lot. They were able to get the trade worked out and bring it to San Jose. I received a more than reasonable trade on my 2012 GMC Acadia Denali and the price was right on the new Range Rover. This was the best sales experience I have ever had in purchasing a new vehicle. I love my new Range Rover! I would highly recommend Land Rover of San Jose to anyone interested in purchasing a new Range River.</Text>

My experience today was exactly what I was looking for when I started looking at the RRS over a year ago.  Unfortunately, my purchase was less than a 1 star rating from management and sales.

Manning Reyes the Service Manager took care of my initial issue that happened a day after I purchased my RRS, and it has been over a month.  If all it took was talking with the Service Manager that day, I could have saved a whole lot of personal time and frustration.

Long story short, I bought my vehicle and discovered a bird dropping that had ruined the paint on the passenger door.  After returning to the dealership for the 3rd time, they attempted to buff it out, but was not successful.  At that time not once did anyone step and offer to take care of this!  After spending 90K, you would think that they would love to do the right thing. Well, I contacted Land Rover North America, and they were less than happy and said, you paid a lot for your vehicle and you should not have to deal with this.  They may be independently owned but they still represent the company, and told me to take to any dealer of my choice.

The GM wanted me to drive the car down again for a 4th time so he could look at my vehicle, where was he when I drove it down?  I bought my car with 21 miles and now I have 1300 miles on it and believe me it is not joy ride miles it is due to multiple trips to their dealership! After my purchase Friday night they told me they would deliver it to me in Sonoma the next day. Well, that never happen Titus called and told me that they did not have a driver! Really? They should throw in some kind of compensation for all issues I have had.  I will be talking to Land Rover NA again and I will praise Manny, but the others need to be evaluated.

After paying out of pocket to correct the bird dropping the detailer noticed that there was also a crack in the back quarter panel!  You have got to be kidding me?  It is a black vehicle and it is hard to notice those exterior flaws if one does not take a fine comb, which at both times I purchased and bought the vehicle home at night.  I guess my expectations were just too high.

My service appointment at Marin land rover was outstanding too!  He ordered the quarter panel and apologized for all the trouble I have had since the purchase.  I will be taking it there moving forward for any service I may need in the future.

Back to Manny Reyes, Stevens Creek Land Rover are very lucky to have you on their team. If I could go back I would pick Manning to buy the vehicle from!

Manny you are the true definition of customer service and are very knowledgeable about what you do, you need a promotion or a raise!< /review>

<Review>There is something new afoot at this dealership, and it may be a good time to buy a car from them.  I just bought my XE 2017 35t, or as some call it the 'baby' F type.  I am pretty giddy about the purchase, and just had a phenomenal drive thru Skyline thru Page Mill, Palo Alto...sweaty palms and all...and car took it all and gave back a LOT.  This car looks great, but also it is humble on the outside as a luxury car, and packs a monster under the hood.  Keeps it real for me.  I don't want too showy.  But the brand is HUGE.  I only say it because of reactions from neighbors.

Now about the dealership.... Energized by totally new models of this revamped, British car company, this dealership is remaking its image too.  I know because i interacted with their new GM, Eric Quistgard, at their performance event earlier this year, and during my purchase.   He also mentioned a new building coming up.  This extreme makeover work-in-progress means that they are eager to prove themselves, especially as the brand is the underdog and the new models are poised for mass market.  Frankly, i really dislike the usual haggling process, and i had none of that for my new, pre-ordered car. they were fair, and also, i was prompt in getting the car as soon as it arrived.  Why not 5 stars ... cause it took a while from the time the deal was agreed upon to get my delivery specialist tour.

Top marks to Eric as the GM  for personally overseeing my sales process and to Jesus for the patient delivery tour.  Why did i write this lengthy review? When i watch football and my team is not playing, i route for the underdog.  Both the dealership and the product have impressed me.  I waited a long time to find the right car.  There is merit here, and it deserves winning.

<Rating>1</Rating><text>Long due review.
This is written after owning a Range Rover for a year.
I purchased a 2012 CPO Range Rover Evoque a year ago from Land Rover San Jose. As with most dealers the purchase was smooth and quick.
The dealership itself is old, and ragged.. they could invest in updating the interior. During my last visit, they had desks lined up in the showroom!
Problems started after one week of purchase when I noticed a high wind noise coming from the driver side mirror or window. I took the car back and complained about the noise. They kept it for a few days and came back with, we could not find anything.
I took the car for a drive with the manager and I pointed out the noise, and he said he doesn't think this is abnormal. He told me to drive the car for a few weeks, and understand what are its normal characteristics, and if I still have problems I can bring it in whenever I want since the car is still under warranty until 2018.
A few months later when it was time to service the car. I brought it in, and still complained about the noise. They said they fixed and they replaced one of the plastic windshield frames.
I drove the car to texas and back and the car still had the noise.
After almost a year, I contacted the head office of land rover. I took the car in, they wanted to charge me for the inspection, said the car's factory warranty is expired and now I am under the extended warranty which doesn't cover body noises.
I talked to the manager, and he started telling me that he has to pay his mechanics, and that they are just a franchise, they are not Land Rover. I was stunned, I did not expect that attitude at all from a "luxury" brand.
They agreed to do it "in good will", the term itself annoyed me because I was complaining from this specific issue for almost a year. Same story, they couldn't hear the noise, until 2 weeks of going back and forth, I took the car for a drive with the mechanic and he heard the noise and finally acknowledged it.
They kept the car for a month, and they managed to fix it eventually. Though they did not offer a discount on the service or tried to make feel better about the whole experience. It seems that they are struggling financially, which is very sad.

I was very disappointed with the overall attitude, and the care. It seems like they have no idea what good customer service is, or how to keep a customer happy.
I decided to sell the car, went to see if they would like to buy it back, they gave me the lowest price compared to any other dealer. Even though they know the history of the car pretty well.
The carfax of the car reported a rollback in the odometer which was, according to the salesman Jeronimo, a human mistake. I recall I reported this earlier and they said they will fix it. A year later I found htat they did not, and lied to me.
Because of that many purchasers were skeptic about the car, until I filed a dispute with carfax and removed the entry.
I have nothing against the car itself. My concern was about dealing with a dealership that didn't take responsibility for their cars, and wondered how would they act if there was a more serious problem. After all the most important part of the car is the after sales experience and servicing.
I have finally sold the car, and bought a more reliable Japanese car.
My advise is stay away from that place, and possibly the whole brand.<//text>< Pics>

<Rate>5< /Rate><Review>I was very impressed with Dr. Lee and his staff.  They were very professional, efficient and friendly.  The office was very clean and they adhere to all safety precautions during the current Coronavirus pandemic which really helped put my mind at ease.

In addition, they have a parking structure, at no charge, that provides ample parking and each level has direct access to the building.

I had to get a root canal retreatment on 01/29/21 of my front upper right tooth (also known as the #8 tooth).  In addition, I had developed an infection above the tooth that needed to be cleaned out as well.  It had been over 30 years since my last root canal and had to be completely redone.  Dr. Lee was very patient and thorough in discussing all of the 3 options as to how to accomplish this.  And while the option I chose meant that the whole process would overall take longer than I would have hoped, it also provided me with the best chance of success in getting it fixed right in one shot rather than repeated procedures.

With any dental surgery there is always the fear of pain, and especially how much one might experience.  During the procedure I did not experience any pain aside from the 2 stings of when he injected the Novocain which is to be expected.  In less than an hour, he had completed the procedure including the cleaning out of the infection.  As I was checking out, he even provided Ibuprophen to help with the swelling and pain that eventually did come after the Novocain wore off.  However, I was already prepared for this since I knew he had had to go deeper to clear out all of the infection.  The pain throughout the weekend was easily managed by Ibuprophen, and as I write this 3 days later, I am back to normal.

I truly appreciated Dr. Lee and his staff for all of their help in fixing my tooth and highly recommend them if you are in need of an excellent Endodontist!< /Review>< pics>

So far, I like it a lot.  It would be nice if they had longer weekend hours.  Early Saturday morning is my favorite workout time.  I have a black card membership, and their hydrotherapy massage tables are wonderful after a workout. < text>
Overall, this place is okay. What hurts the rating is the service. The food is okay.

Food:
New England Clam Chowder in a bowl was good. It has a milky taste. Bread wasn't too sour. The $11 price tag doesn't justify the worth. It taste like any other clam chowder you can get at the Cannery.

The Alaskan Salmon taste like it was frozen. Part of the fish was dry. It didn't taste fishy, which is what I usually worry about in a fish.

The French Dip was okay. Nothing to brag about. The sauce could of been more generous. The meat was good. Not too dry.

Service:
The server Tyler is quick to get our order. Our drinks came out at a reasonable time. Our food, however took forever... I believe they forgot about us since we saw people who came after us got their food. The food felt warm. Not hot.

Price:
It was pricey for what it was. For the price I paid, I would expect better service or better food. Both were lacking. Beer will set you $7-9 bucks a glass. Sandwiches are in the $13-$20. Special entries are about $15-$25.

Ambience:
This place feels cozy. Has a bar vibe. Plenty of seats. Lots of televisions that have multiple games running. There are a quite a few vehicle decors located throughout the restaurant. There is a dance floor and stage for performances.<//text>

<username>Nikki Gonzales<//username><pics>None<//pics><userid>108682024533243002460<//userid><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Upon entering this restaurant while on a trip to monterey, i quickly pulled out my phone to check out the reviews. I was shocked to see the long list of bad reviews for this restaurant. Still i sat down and thought I'd give it a chance. I'm happy i did. Right away, i was greeted by a waiter with a menu. He was super friendly and kind. He came back with drinks and took our orders almost immediately. My friend ordered a burger and fries while i ordered the clam chowder bread bowl. The food was ready very fast and was served hot and delicious. There were no problems with the food and the order was perfect. The waiter made a habit of stopping by to make sure we were okay and ask if we needed anything. He constantly refilled our drinks and was very polite. The burger was enormous and the clam chowder bread bowl was of good size. The restrooms were clean and the music was nice. The bill was $30 for a party of two, which is pretty typical for a casual restaurant on cannery row.<//Review>

On the plus side the kids food was above a little above average.  Also, our friend reported his red snapper sandwich was pretty good.  And the onion rings weren't bad.

<Date>1531620169688<//Date><Review>AWFUL SERVICE
For being so expensive you'd think you could get decent service. A steak, a burger, and a margarita came out to $60 something dollars, which I wouldn't have minded if I could've gotten anything close to a decent service.

I ordered the bacon cheeseburger, specifically asked for it to be extra extra extra well done, no tomato, add grilled onion.
They brought the steak out about 10 minutes before the burger, so by the time I got my food, the person I was with was already half way done with their food. No biggie.
They eventually brought my burger, no grilled onions, lots of tomato. Bit irritating, but again not that big of a deal. What really got me was when I cut into it and saw that it was pink ALL THE WAY THROUGH. Which absolutely disgusted me. The food took so long to come in the first place (wasn't very busy at all) that I didn't want to sit there and wait for it to be recooked, because again, the person I was with was almost done at this point. I didn't say anything (one because it just seemed pointless, two because I'm a server as well and I didn't feel like being difficult) but I definitely couldn't eat it, just gave it to the person I was with and just ate the maybe 8 or so french fries that came with it. I shouldn't have been so shocked that she got everything so wrong, seeing as she didn't even have a pen and pad to write the order down. Guess she thought she could memorize it? She either thought wrong or just didn't care. I then had to ask THREE SEPERATE SERVERS to get ketchup and napkins for the fries. I was so disgusted with this place. As I was walking out the door, I was discussing how terrible the experience was with the person I was with, and I said something along the lines of "that was awful". A random woman on the sidewalk outside overheard, looked at us and said "OMG I know. I went there for the first time last week. Terrible service right?"
I thought maybe it was just a bad day for them, guess that's just the regular there.
The ONLY pleasant things about this restaurant were the live music and the manager. The two men playing and singing were great, and though the server never bothered to come check on us, the manager did and he was very helpful and friendly. Even offered to take our drink order, and helped up chose a drink with a great recommendation. Shout out to you guys for being the only part of this experience that didn't absolutely disgust me.

ABSOLUTELY RIDICULOUS
SAVE YOUR MONEY, RUN
NEVER AGAIN</Review></record></dataset><record>

<Rating>3< /Rating>< Text>
Monterey is beautiful with many restaurants offering exquisite dining experiences that live up to Monterey's class. Unfortunately, that was not our experience today at Sly McFly's. The wait staff was well below standard for the prices on the menu...if you're going to be in a high touristy area and have prices that are high for lunch, then you need to have experienced waitstaff that fit the venue. Our waiter seemed very distracted and disinterested in serving us, nor did he know much about the menu or food. It took over an hour to get our meals which made our little one's upset and bored, making them hangry and difficult to tame. When the food came 2 out of 3 meals were wrong.
